msg:Overall it's good, but there is no underground parking lot. If you have luggage, you need to walk a distance. The ground parking lot is relatively small and has charging piles.
The room is relatively simple, with a sink design, no place to put on makeup, a trash can on one side and a towel rack on the other. The bathroom is relatively spacious. The air conditioning is also sufficient, and the room is very warm. It's just that the air conditioning is not turned on when visiting the exhibition and the library, which is a bit cold, because you have to go outside or walk through the library to get from the room to the hot spring.
There are four hot spring pools open, not many people, not many children, the overall experience is very good, you can take pictures, and there are fruit biscuits and snacks.
The sizzling chicken feet and fish are not bad, there are tiger skin chicken feet and grilled fish. The spinach noodle bowl is really big.
